[Sunday, 28 August 2016 at 16:31:01]
116
*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

*Admins: flood settings*

`/antiflood` = manage the flood settings in private, with an inline keyboard. You can change the sensitivity, the action (kick/ban), and even set some exceptions.
`/antiflood [number]` = set how many messages a user can write in 5 seconds.
_Note_ : the number must be higher than 3 and lower than 26.

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: media settings*

`/media` = receive in PM an inline keyboard to change all the media settings.
`/warnmax media [number]` = set the max number of warnings before be kicked/banned for have sent a forbidden media.
`/nowarns (by reply)` = reset the number of warnings for the users (*NOTE: both regular warnings and media warnings*).
`/media list` = show the current settings for all the media.

*List of supported media*: _image, audio, video, sticker, gif, voice, contact, file, link_


[Wednesday, 31 August 2016 at 13:15:26]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

116
*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: special characters*

`/menu` = you will receive in private the menu keyboard.
Here you will find two particular options: _Arab and RTL_.

*Arab*: when Arab it's not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone who will write an arab character will be kicked from the group.
*Rtl*: it stands for 'Righ To Left' character, and it's the responsible of the weird service messages that are written in the opposite sense.
When Rtl is not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone that writes this character (or that has it in his name) will be kicked.

*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

[Wednesday, 31 August 2016 at 20:09:12]
116
*Admins: links*

`/setlink [link|'no']` = set the group link, so it can be re-called by other admins, or unset it.
`/link` = get the group link, if set by the owner.

*Note*: the bot can recognize valid group links. If a link is not valid, you won't receive a reply.

[Wednesday, 31 August 2016 at 20:09:12]
116
*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Wednesday, 31 August 2016 at 20:09:21]
116
*Admins: group language*

`/lang` = choose the group language (can be changed in private too).


[Wednesday, 31 August 2016 at 20:09:33]
116
*Admins: media settings*

`/media` = receive in PM an inline keyboard to change all the media settings.
`/warnmax media [number]` = set the max number of warnings before be kicked/banned for have sent a forbidden media.
`/nowarns (by reply)` = reset the number of warnings for the users (*NOTE: both regular warnings and media warnings*).
`/media list` = show the current settings for all the media.

*List of supported media*: _image, audio, video, sticker, gif, voice, contact, file, link_


[Wednesday, 31 August 2016 at 20:09:34]

`/help` : show this message.

116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

[Thursday, 01 September 2016 at 12:55:28]
116
*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

[Thursday, 01 September 2016 at 12:55:35]

*Admins: group settings*

`/menu` = manage the group settings in private with an handy inline keyboard.
`/report [on/off]` (by reply) = the user won't be able (_off_) or will be able (_on_) to use "@admin" command.

*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Sunday, 04 September 2016 at 09:20:46]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

[Monday, 05 September 2016 at 00:49:23]

*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`

*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

[Monday, 05 September 2016 at 01:38:49]
116
*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

[Tuesday, 06 September 2016 at 06:59:07]
116
*Admins: media settings*

`/media` = receive in PM an inline keyboard to change all the media settings.
`/warnmax media [number]` = set the max number of warnings before be kicked/banned for have sent a forbidden media.
`/nowarns (by reply)` = reset the number of warnings for the users (*NOTE: both regular warnings and media warnings*).
`/media list` = show the current settings for all the media.

*List of supported media*: _image, audio, video, sticker, gif, voice, contact, file, link_

[Tuesday, 06 September 2016 at 09:33:35]
116
*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group

`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

[Wednesday, 07 September 2016 at 16:34:56]
116
*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

[Wednesday, 07 September 2016 at 16:35:00]
116
*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

Selamat Datang Di Group kedua Main WW Indonesia.

Hal yang paling wajib sebelum bermain adalah add moderatorbot :
@werewolfbot
@werewolfIIbot 

Bahasa Moderator Group ini yaitu Bahasa Inggris (English)

â€¢Untuk merubah Bahasa Moderator Bot (Personal) ketik /setlang kemudian pilih Bahasa yang diinginkan.

â€¢Untuk mengetahui penjelasan role dan cara bermain , Klik [MWI](http://goo.gl/UWCQqm) atau ketik /rolelist

â€¢Klik [RULES]( http://goo.gl/7HhUug) atau ketik /rules atau #rules untuk mengetahui Peraturan bermain di @mainwerewolfindo

â€¢Untuk info lebih lanjut bisa diliat di @balaidesa

Kebiasaan group ini capslock - rusuh - flood - kompor - micin. Jadi siapkan mental dan jangan baper :)

ğŸ’•LOVERS SEASONğŸ’•
=====================
=======RULES========

ğŸ’–  Lovers harus "bertahan hidup" dan "menang" hingga permainan berakhir
ğŸ’–  Role apapun (yang dipasangkan) diperbolehkan
ğŸ’–  Cupid yang memasangkan pemain lain tidak diperkenankan menspoiler siapa yang menjadi lovers (break the rule will get you warn [1~3])
ğŸ’–  Cupid diperbolehkan memasangkan diri sendiri
ğŸ’–  Event dinyatakan aktif apabila pemain yang /join telah mencapai sama dengan atau lebih dari (=/>)  25 orang
ğŸ’–  Waktu permainan harus dalam on-air event
ğŸ’–  SS tidak boleh di cut atau di block (break the rule will get you warn [1~3])
ğŸ’–  Harus bermain di grup Werewolf Micin Indonesia


Semangat!! ğŸ˜ğŸ˜ğŸ˜ğŸ˜
Selamat bermain dan berjuang bersama pasanganmu, Lovers Micin Indonesia!!

*Admins: links*

`/setlink [link|'no']` = set the group link, so it can be re-called by other admins, or unset it.
`/link` = get the group link, if set by the owner.

*Note*: the bot can recognize valid group links. If a link is not valid, you won't receive a reply.

[Thursday, 08 September 2016 at 17:50:04]
116
*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Thursday, 08 September 2016 at 17:56:10]
116
*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions

[Friday, 09 September 2016 at 10:58:56]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

116
*Admins: flood settings*

`/antiflood` = manage the flood settings in private, with an inline keyboard. You can change the sensitivity, the action (kick/ban), and even set some exceptions.
`/antiflood [number]` = set how many messages a user can write in 5 seconds.
_Note_ : the number must be higher than 3 and lower than 26.

116
*Admins: media settings*

`/media` = receive in PM an inline keyboard to change all the media settings.
`/warnmax media [number]` = set the max number of warnings before be kicked/banned for have sent a forbidden media.
`/nowarns (by reply)` = reset the number of warnings for the users (*NOTE: both regular warnings and media warnings*).
`/media list` = show the current settings for all the media.

*List of supported media*: _image, audio, video, sticker, gif, voice, contact, file, link_

â€¢ I can detect global banned users and not let them enter my groups
â€¢ You can *kick or ban* users (even in normal groups) by reply/username
â€¢ Set rules and a description
â€¢ Turn on a configurable *anti-flood* system
â€¢ Customize the *welcome message*, also with gif and stickers
â€¢ Warn users, and kick/ban them if they reach a max number of warns
â€¢ Warn or kick users if they send a specific media
...and more, below you can find the "all commands" button to get the whole list!

You can manage the group flood settings from here.

*1st row*
â€¢ *ON/OFF*: the current status of the anti-flood
â€¢ *Kick/Ban*: what to do when someone is flooding

*2nd row*
â€¢ you can use *+/-* to change the current sensitivity of the anti-flood system
â€¢ the number is the max number of messages that can be sent in _5 seconds_
â€¢ max value: _25_ - min value: _4_

*3rd row* and below
You can set some exceptions for the anti-flood:
â€¢ âœ…: the media will be ignored by the anti-flood
â€¢ âŒ: the media won't be ignored by the anti-flood
â€¢ *Note*: in "_texts_" are included all the other types of media (file, audio...)

Hey, *ï¼ (\*^ï½ª^)ï¼ *!
I'm a bot created to help manage Werewolf groups which use @werewolfbot.

*What can I do for you?*
Wew, I have a lot of useful tools!
â€¢ I can detect global banned users and not let them enter my groups
â€¢ You can *kick or ban* users (even in normal groups) by reply/username
â€¢ Set rules and a description
â€¢ Turn on a configurable *anti-flood* system
â€¢ Customize the *welcome message*, also with gif and stickers
â€¢ Warn users, and kick/ban them if they reach a max number of warns
â€¢ Warn or kick users if they send a specific media
...and more, below you can find the "all commands" button to get the whole list!

To use me, *you need to add me as administrator of the group*, or Telegram won't let me work properly! (if you have some doubts about this, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/63))
You can report bugs/send feedbacks/ask a question to my creator just using "`!<feedback>`".

*Moderatori: messaggio di benvenuto*

`/menu` = ricevi in privato la tastiera del menu. LÃ¬ troverai un'opzione per abilitare/disabilitare il messaggio di benvenuto.

*Messaggio di benvenuto personalizzato:*
`/welcome Benvenuto $name, benvenuto nel gruppo!`
Scrivi dopo "/welcome" il tuo benvenuto personalizzato. Puoi usare dei segnaposto per includere nome/username/id del nuovo membro del gruppo
Segnaposto: _$username_ (verrÃ  sostituito con lo username); _$name_ (verrÃ  sostituito col nome); _$id_ (verrÃ  sostituito con l'id); _$title_ (verrÃ  sostituito con il nome del gruppo).

*GIF/sticker come messaggio di benvenuto*
Puoi usare una gif/uno sticker per dare il benvenuto ai nuovi membri. Per impostare la gif/sticker, invialo e rispondigli con '/welcome'

*Messaggio di benvenuto composto*
Puoi comporre il messaggio di benvenuto con le regole, la descrizione e la lista dei moderatori.
Per comporlo, scrivi `/welcome` seguito dai codici di cosa vuoi includere nel messaggio.
_Codici_ : *r* = regole; *a* = descrizione (about); *m* = moderatori.
Ad esempio, con "`/welcome rm`"il messaggio di benvenuto mostrerÃ  regole e moderatori

116
*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

[Monday, 12 September 2016 at 09:27:13]

118
*New description:*
"Werewolf

Setiap malam werewolf punya kekuatan untuk memilih salah satu player untuk dimakan, namun bisa juga memilih tidak memakan siapapun agar tidak dicurigai.

Seer

Seer adalah paranormal. Jadi dia diberikan opsi oleh@werewolfbot, setiap malam dia bisa memilih salah satu player untuk dibuka identitasnya, lalu @werewolfbot akan PM identitas orang yang dipilih jika ternyata werewolf, yang jadi seer memiliki 2 kemungkinan. Seer bisa memberitahu yang lain namun resiko akan ketahuan dia yang jadi seer, lalu keesokan malam, wolf pasti akan makan player yang jadi seer tersebut. Atau seer juga bisa memilih berkomplot dengan beholder.

Beholder

Yang jadi beholder akan mengetahui siapa yang jadi seer. Tugas utamanya dia harus berkomplot dengan seer mempengaruhi player lain untuk bunuh wolf.

Harlot/Slut

Harlot adalah peran yang sangat gak bermoral namun seringkali berguna. Dia adalah pelacur/WTS di desa. Kerjaannya tiap malam mengunjung salah satu player untuk bekimpoi. Jika yang dikunjungi warga biasa maka keesokan harinya dia masih hidup lalu muncul notikasi PM dari @werewolfbot kurang lebih â€œsemalam kamu mengunjungi player Y lalu bercinta dengan keras. Esok paginya kamu menyelinap keluarÂ diam-diam, kamuÂ puas menikmati semalam bersama player Y. Namun jika yang dikunjungi adalah player yang jadi wolf, maka harlot akan mati. Selanjutnya muncul notifikasi kurang lebih â€œPlayer X adalah harlot. Semalam dia salah berkimpoi mengunjungi player yang ternyata werewolf. Tubuhnya ditemukan tercabik-cabik. Mau dapat kepuasan duniawi malah matiâ€ Jadi harlot bisa bantu warga, berkoar-koar kalau semalam dia kunjungi si Z yang ternyata wolf.

Khusus skenario harlot ini kadang bahasa inggrisnya tidak pantas yah, jadi jangan terlalu diimajinasikan. Hehehe

Gunner

Yang jadi gunner punya kesempatan 2x untuk menembak player yang dicurigai sebagai wolf. Namun jangan sampai ketahuan kamu gunner karena malam berikutnya pasti gunner yang dimangsa wolf.

Detektif

Tugas detektif kurang lebih sama dengan Seer. Tiap malam dia bisa pilih orang untuk dibuka identitasnya. Namun kerjanya independent, tidak dibantu beholder. Yang jadi detektif jangan ketahuan wolf, awas dimakan.

Lowly Villager

Lowly Villager hanya rakyat jelata yang tidak punya kekuatan spesial. Dia hanya bisa menghasut dan mempengaruhi player lain tanpa bukti apapun. Namun Lowly Villager bisa direkrut menjadi cultist.

Cultist

Pernah dengar Lia Eden yang merekrut orang untuk jadi pengikut ajaran sesatnya. Cultist kurang lebih seperti itu. Tiap malam cultist memilih player lain untuk direkrut. Cultist sebenarnya musuh wolf sekaligus musuh warga. Kenapa? karena diakhir permainan saat semua wolf mati dengan kondisi mayoritas yang tersisa adalah cultist, warga dinyatakan kalah dan cultist yang menang. Saya pribadi, ada kepuasan tersendiri saat menjadi cultist dan akhirnya menang.

Cultist Hunter

Berbeda dengan gunner. Tugas cutist hunter tiap malam mencari player yang dicurigai sebagai cultist untuk selanjutnya dibunuh agar populasi cultist habis tak bersisa.

Traitor

Traitor awalnyaÂ adalahÂ warga biasa yang tidak punya kekuatan spesial. Namun saat semua wolf mati, traitor akan berubah otomatis menjadi wolf (dia berkhianat kepada warga).

Drunk

Drunk disini kerjanya hanya tukang mabuk. Satu-satunya kelebihan yang dia miliki, jika wolf datang untuk makan drunk, maka drunk akan mati. Namun memberikan efek ke wolf menjadi ikutan mabuk sehingga wolf tidak bisa makan orang.

Wild Child

Wild Child disini ibaratnya anak angkat. Di awal permainan Wild Child harus memilih salah satu player untuk dijadikan orang tua. Jika orang tua wild child mati, maka wild child akan "marah" dan otomatis berubah jadi wolf.

Cursed

Cursed disini adalah player yang terkutuk. Jika wolf makan cursed, wolfnya mati lalu cursed akan berubah jadi wolf.

The Fool

Peran The Fool hanya ada diÂ chaos mode. Cara masuk ke chaos mode ketik \startchaos

The Fool akan diberikan notifikasi oleh bot bahwa dia adalah Seer. Dia sebenarnya tidak punya kemampuan paranormal seperti Seer asli. Fool hanya akan membingungkan"

[Monday, 12 September 2016 at 17:59:17]

*Admins: links*

`/setlink [link|'no']` = set the group link, so it can be re-called by other admins, or unset it.
`/link` = get the group link, if set by the owner.

*Note*: the bot can recognize valid group links. If a link is not valid, you won't receive a reply.

*Admins: media settings*

`/media` = receive in PM an inline keyboard to change all the media settings.
`/warnmax media [number]` = set the max number of warnings before be kicked/banned for have sent a forbidden media.
`/nowarns (by reply)` = reset the number of warnings for the users (*NOTE: both regular warnings and media warnings*).
`/media list` = show the current settings for all the media.

*List of supported media*: _image, audio, video, sticker, gif, voice, contact, file, link_

*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

Hey, *\*\*~~Ali*!
I'm a bot created to help manage Werewolf groups which use @werewolfbot.

*What can I do for you?*
Wew, I have a lot of useful tools!
â€¢ I can detect global banned users and not let them enter my groups
â€¢ You can *kick or ban* users (even in normal groups) by reply/username
â€¢ Set rules and a description
â€¢ Turn on a configurable *anti-flood* system
â€¢ Customize the *welcome message*, also with gif and stickers
â€¢ Warn users, and kick/ban them if they reach a max number of warns
â€¢ Warn or kick users if they send a specific media
...and more, below you can find the "all commands" button to get the whole list!

To use me, *you need to add me as administrator of the group*, or Telegram won't let me work properly! (if you have some doubts about this, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/63))
You can report bugs/send feedbacks/ask a question to my creator just using "`!<feedback>`".

*Admins: flood settings*

`/antiflood` = manage the flood settings in private, with an inline keyboard. You can change the sensitivity, the action (kick/ban), and even set some exceptions.
`/antiflood [number]` = set how many messages a user can write in 5 seconds.
_Note_ : the number must be higher than 3 and lower than 26.

116
*Admins: special characters*

`/menu` = you will receive in private the menu keyboard.
Here you will find two particular options: _Arab and RTL_.

*Arab*: when Arab it's not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone who will write an arab character will be kicked from the group.
*Rtl*: it stands for 'Righ To Left' character, and it's the responsible of the weird service messages that are written in the opposite sense.
When Rtl is not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone that writes this character (or that has it in his name) will be kicked.

116
*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

116
You can manage the group flood settings from here.

*1st row*
â€¢ *ON/OFF*: the current status of the anti-flood
â€¢ *Kick/Ban*: what to do when someone is flooding

*2nd row*
â€¢ you can use *+/-* to change the current sensitivity of the anti-flood system
â€¢ the number is the max number of messages that can be sent in _5 seconds_
â€¢ max value: _25_ - min value: _4_

*3rd row* and below
You can set some exceptions for the anti-flood:
â€¢ âœ…: the media will be ignored by the anti-flood
â€¢ âŒ: the media won't be ignored by the anti-flood
â€¢ *Note*: in "_texts_" are included all the other types of media (file, audio...)

116
*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

[Thursday, 15 September 2016 at 08:38:31]

*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

*Moderatori: linguaggio del bot*

`/lang` = scegli la lingua del bot (puÃ² essere cambiata anche in privato).

*Nota*: i traduttori sono utenti volontari, quindi non posso assicurare la correttezza delle traduzioni. E non posso costringerli a tradurre le nuove stringhe dopo un aggiornamento (le stringhe non tradotte saranno in inglese).
Comunque, chiunque puÃ² tradurre il bot. Usa il comando `/strings` per ricevere un file _.lua_ con tutte le stringhe (in inglese).
Usa `/strings [codice lingua]` per ricevere il file associato alla lingua richiesta (esempio: _/strings es_ ).
Nel file troverai tutte le istruzioni: seguile, e il linguggio sarÃ  disponibile il prima possibile ;)  (traduzione in italiano NON NECESSARIA)

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Monday, 19 September 2016 at 06:06:57]

*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

[Monday, 19 September 2016 at 10:09:15]

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: flood settings*

`/antiflood` = manage the flood settings in private, with an inline keyboard. You can change the sensitivity, the action (kick/ban), and even set some exceptions.
`/antiflood [number]` = set how many messages a user can write in 5 seconds.
_Note_ : the number must be higher than 3 and lower than 26.


[Monday, 19 September 2016 at 13:17:27]
116
*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Monday, 19 September 2016 at 14:42:53]
116
*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

[Monday, 19 September 2016 at 14:43:07]
116
*Admins: media settings*

`/media` = receive in PM an inline keyboard to change all the media settings.
`/warnmax media [number]` = set the max number of warnings before be kicked/banned for have sent a forbidden media.
`/nowarns (by reply)` = reset the number of warnings for the users (*NOTE: both regular warnings and media warnings*).
`/media list` = show the current settings for all the media.

*List of supported media*: _image, audio, video, sticker, gif, voice, contact, file, link_

You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

[Monday, 19 September 2016 at 14:43:25]
116
*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: info about the group*

`/setrules [group rules]` = set the new rules for the group (the old ones will be overwritten).
`/addrules [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing rules.
`/setabout [group description]` = set a new description for the group (the old one will be overwritten).
`/addabout [text]` = add some text at the end of the existing description.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Tuesday, 20 September 2016 at 07:15:50]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

[Tuesday, 20 September 2016 at 07:15:54]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

[Tuesday, 20 September 2016 at 07:15:59]
116
*Admins: special characters*

`/menu` = you will receive in private the menu keyboard.
Here you will find two particular options: _Arab and RTL_.

*Arab*: when Arab it's not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone who will write an arab character will be kicked from the group.
*Rtl*: it stands for 'Righ To Left' character, and it's the responsible of the weird service messages that are written in the opposite sense.
When Rtl is not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone that writes this character (or that has it in his name) will be kicked.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

[Tuesday, 20 September 2016 at 07:16:21]
116
*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

[Tuesday, 20 September 2016 at 07:16:32]
116
*Admins: special characters*

`/menu` = you will receive in private the menu keyboard.
Here you will find two particular options: _Arab and RTL_.

*Arab*: when Arab it's not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone who will write an arab character will be kicked from the group.
*Rtl*: it stands for 'Righ To Left' character, and it's the responsible of the weird service messages that are written in the opposite sense.
When Rtl is not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone that writes this character (or that has it in his name) will be kicked.

[Tuesday, 20 September 2016 at 07:35:59]
116
*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

!echo *PIN & EDITPIN COMMAND*
!pin<spasi>text 
- untuk pesan yang biasanya di jadikan pin message

!editpin<spasi>text yang baru
- ngedit pesan (pinned message) , auto edit tanpa di reply lagi sama bot

!pin<spasi>tanpa text
- untuk mengetahui pin msg yang udah di set, nanti bot nya nge-reply
(kayak command /player di moderator bot)
jadi kalo mau nge-pinned message, cukup tekan *!pin*

*DEEPLINK ($rules)*
- penjelasan -
Ini hyperlink, tapi kalo di klik, bakal ngarah ke arenabot, dan waktu user klik tombol "start" , bot akan balas rules group

Penggunaan: di !extra & !welcome
*jangan gunakan di rules , karena dia emang link ke rules*

ğŸ‘‡ğŸ‘‡
Contoh â€”> "[ini link rules]($rules)"

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Wednesday, 21 September 2016 at 17:41:22]
116

*Admins: flood settings*

`/antiflood` = manage the flood settings in private, with an inline keyboard. You can change the sensitivity, the action (kick/ban), and even set some exceptions.
`/antiflood [number]` = set how many messages a user can write in 5 seconds.
_Note_ : the number must be higher than 3 and lower than 26.

*Admins: flood settings*

[Wednesday, 21 September 2016 at 18:49:15]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

[Wednesday, 21 September 2016 at 18:49:19]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

[Wednesday, 21 September 2016 at 18:49:23]
116
*Admins: links*

`/setlink [link|'no']` = set the group link, so it can be re-called by other admins, or unset it.
`/link` = get the group link, if set by the owner.

*Note*: the bot can recognize valid group links. If a link is not valid, you won't receive a reply.

[Wednesday, 21 September 2016 at 18:49:26]
116
*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Admins: special characters*

`/menu` = you will receive in private the menu keyboard.
Here you will find two particular options: _Arab and RTL_.

*Arab*: when Arab it's not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone who will write an arab character will be kicked from the group.
*Rtl*: it stands for 'Righ To Left' character, and it's the responsible of the weird service messages that are written in the opposite sense.
When Rtl is not allowed (ğŸš«), everyone that writes this character (or that has it in his name) will be kicked.

116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

116
*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

RULES GAME WEREWOLF :

1. WAJIB memasang display picture, username, dan nama yang DAPAT DIBACA dan DIPAHAMI member lain. Tidak mengandung unsur SARA, Pornografi, Celaan, Kekerasan, HANYA emoji, serta foto yang menyinggung dengan sengaja (termasuk memasang foto moderator).

PASTIKAN SEBELUM ANDA JOIN TIDAK MEMILIKI KEWAJIBAN YANG HARUS DILAKUKAN SAAT PERMAINAN BERLANGSUNG.

6. DILARANG WASIAT / UP MAUPUN MENGINGATKAN WASIAT SETELAH MATI.  Signal / human error adalah konsekuensi pemain.
7. JALANKAN PERAN DENGAN SEBAIKBAIKNYA. DILARANG berkhianat sehingga menyebabkan rekan setimnya kalah. 
Kecuali :
-mason yang ingin mengumumkan rekannya
-lovers diperbolehkan mengkhianati timnya demi kemenangan lovers
-cupid tidak boleh membeberkan pasangannya di publik
8. DILARANG minta rekrut untuk berpindah role, seperti minta gigit dan minta convert cult bagi untuk SEMUA ROLE.
9. Dilarang COPAS Pesan/Screen Capture/Forward/GIF dari WEREWOLF BOT maupun PLAYER LAIN ke group.
10. DILARANG minta PM role tertentu di group.   contoh: "Seer PM saya" kecuali minta cek.
Serta DILARANG PM mengenai game yang sedang berlangsung SETELAH MATI.
11. Diperbolehkan PM dengan ketentuan berada dalam 1 tim, dan mengetahui ROLE orang yang akan di PM dengan PASTI, seperti:
-Beholder PM SEER (bukan diumumin di grup)
-Pemain yang telah dicek SEER dan DETEKTIF (termasuk mason).
-Sesama mason, werewolf, cultist, lover.

-Beholder PM SEER (bukan diumumin di grup)

`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

*Admins: extra commands*

`/extra [#trigger] [reply]` = set a reply to be sent when someone writes the trigger.
_Example_ : with "`/extra #hello Good morning!`", the bot will reply "Good morning!" each time someone writes #hello.
You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Saturday, 24 September 2016 at 08:16:33]

You can reply to a media (_photo, file, vocal, video, gif, audio_) with `/extra #yourtrigger` to save the #extra and receive that media each time you use # command
`/extra list` = get the list of your custom commands.
`/extra del [#trigger]` = delete the trigger and its message.

*Note:* the markdown is supported. If the text sent breaks the markdown, the bot will notify that something is wrong.
For a correct use of the markdown, check [this post](https://telegram.me/GroupButler_ch/46) in the GroupButler channel

[Saturday, 24 September 2016 at 08:16:36]
116
*Admins: flood settings*

`/antiflood` = manage the flood settings in private, with an inline keyboard. You can change the sensitivity, the action (kick/ban), and even set some exceptions.
`/antiflood [number]` = set how many messages a user can write in 5 seconds.
_Note_ : the number must be higher than 3 and lower than 26.

*Admins: links*

`/setlink [link|'no']` = set the group link, so it can be re-called by other admins, or unset it.
`/link` = get the group link, if set by the owner.

*Note*: the bot can recognize valid group links. If a link is not valid, you won't receive a reply.

[Saturday, 24 September 2016 at 10:54:53]
116
*Admins: banhammer powers*

`/kick [by reply|username]` = kick a user from the group (they can be added again).
`/ban [by reply|username]` = ban a user from the group (also from normal groups).
`/tempban [minutes]` = ban an user for a specific amount of minutes (minutes must be < 10.080, one week). For now, only by reply.
`/unban [by reply|username]` = unban the user from the group.
`/user [by reply|username|id]` = returns a two pages messages: the first shows how many times the user has been banned *in all the groups* (divided in sections), the second page shows some general stats about the user: messages/media in the group, warns received and so on.
`/status [username|id]` = show the current status of the user `(member|kicked/left the chat|banned|admin/creator|never seen)`.
`/banlist` = show a list of banned users. Includes the motivations (if given during the ban)
`/banlist -` = clean the banlist.

*Note*: you can write something after `/ban` command (or after the username, if you are banning by username). This comment will be used as the motivation of the ban.

[Saturday, 24 September 2016 at 15:05:59]
116
*Admins: welcome settings*

`/menu` = receive in private the menu keyboard. You will find an option to enable/disable the welcome message.

*Custom welcome message:*
`/welcome Welcome $name, enjoy the group!`
Write after "/welcome" your welcome message. You can use some placeholders to include the name/username/id of the new member of the group
Placeholders: _$username_ (will be replaced with the username); _$name_ (will be replaced with the name); _$id_ (will be replaced with the id); _$title_ (will be replaced with the group title).

*GIF/sticker as welcome message*
You can use a particular gif/sticker as welcome message. To set it, reply to a gif/sticker with '/welcome'

*Composed welcome message*
You can compose your welcome message with the rules, the description and the admin list.
You can compose it by writing `/welcome` followed by the codes of what the welcome message has to include.
_Codes_ : *r* = rules; *a* = description (about); *m* = adminlist.
For example, with "`/welcome rm`", the welcome message will show rules and admin list

116
*Commands for all*:
`/dashboard` : see all the group info from private
`/rules` (if unlocked) : show the group rules
`/about` (if unlocked) : show the group description
`/adminlist` (if unlocked) : show the admins of the group
`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

`@admin` (if unlocked) : by reply = report the message replied to all the admins; no reply (with text) = send a feedback to all the admins
`/kickme` : get kicked by the bot
`/faq` : some useful answers to frequent quetions
`/id` : get the chat id, or the user id if by reply
`/echo [text]` : the bot will send the text back (with markdown, available only in private for non-admin users)
`/info` : show some useful informations about the bot
`/group` or `/support` : get the support group link (if you reply a user with `/support`, I will reply to them)
`!`<feedback> : send a feedback/report a bug/ask a question to my creator. (Example: !Your bot is awesome)
`/help` : show this message.

*Admins: warns*

`/warn [by reply]` = warn a user. Once the max number is reached, he will be kicked/banned.
`/warnmax` = set the max number of the warns before the kick/ban.

How to see how many warns a user has received: the number is showed in the second page of the `/user` command. In this page, you will see a button to reset this number.

[Sunday, 25 September 2016 at 09:55:07]

1. Group rules are simple:
a. Obey the Godfathers (Admins). Their words are final, and you only annoy them more by arguing.
b. Keep it SFW, don't offend other players, no porn, no ads, no spam. Remember, nobody likes a whiner when they got a Tommy Gun.
c. Current settings for media: file, voice, and audio is disallowed. If youstill share it after kicked once, it's banhammer time.
d. No ads, please!
e. Don't Impersonate Bots!

2. Playing rules are simple, too:
a. Don't send any influencing message if you're not in the game.  The Godfather doesn't like any competition.
b. What happens in private, stays private. No forwarding or screenshots of the bot's messages!
c. You can PM everyone in the game, but don't push it.
d. Don't change your name in the middle of a game! The Godfather wants to be able to track each and every one of you.
e. English only, please! We're working on other language for this setting, just you wait.
e.1. For Portuguese/Brazilian Mafia, go to @werewolfmafiabr!
